<s> a hoarse laugh the bargemen exchange remarks a hush again and thomas begins speaking thomas <\s>
<s> we are all in the tepth together and it iss nature that has put us there <\s>
<s> it's london put us there <\s>
<s> it iss not lonton nor it iss not the union it iss nature <\s>
<s> it iss no disgrace whateffer to a potty to give in to nature <\s>
<s> for this nature iss a fery pig thing it is pigger than what a man is <\s>
<s> there iss more years to my hett than to the hett of any one here <\s>
<s> it is fery pat look you this going against nature <\s>
<s> it is pat to make other potties suffer when there is nothing to pe cot py it <\s>
<s> thomas angrily goes on what are ye laughing at <\s>
<s> it is pat i say <\s>
<s> we are fighting for a principle there is no potty that shall say i am not a peliever in principle <\s>
<s> putt when nature says no further then it is no coot snapping your fingers in her face <\s>
<s> a laugh from roberts and murmurs of approval this nature must pe humort <\s>
<s> it is a man's pisiness to pe pure honest just and merciful <\s>
<s> that's what chapel tells you <\s>
<s> to roberts angrily and look you david roberts chapel tells you ye can do that without going against nature <\s>
<s> what about the union <\s>
<s> i ton't trust the union they haf treated us like tirt <\s>
<s> do what we tell you said they <\s>
<s> i haf peen captain of the furnace men twenty years and i say to the union excitedly can you tell me then as well as i can tell you what iss the right wages for the work that these men do <\s>
<s> for fife and twenty years i haf paid my moneys to the union and with great excitement for nothings <\s>
<s> what iss that but roguery for all that this mr <\s>
<s> get on with you <\s>
<s> cut on with it then <\s>
<s> look you if a man toes not trust me am i going to trust him <\s>
<s> let them alone for rogues and act for ourselves <\s>
<s> that's what we been doin haven't we <\s>
<s> with increased excitement i wass brought up to do for meself <\s>
<s> i wass brought up to go without a thing if i hat not moneys to puy it <\s>
<s> there iss too much look you of doing things with other people's moneys <\s>
<s> we haf fought fair and if we haf peen beaten it iss no fault of ours <\s>
<s> gif us the power to make terms with london for ourself if we ton't succeed i say it iss petter to take our peating like men than to tie like togs or hang on to others coat tails to make them do our pisiness for us <\s>
<s> muttering who wants to <\s>
<s> if i stand up to a potty and he knocks me town i am not to go hollering to other potties to help me i am to stand up again and if he knocks me town properly i am to stay there is n't that right <\s>
